<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преобразить.html>преобрази́вший</a> (21721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразить.html>преобрази́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preobrazívšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преобразиться.html>преобрази́ться</a> (15853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразить.html>преобрази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preobrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразиться.html>преобрази́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preobrazítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преображаться.html>преобража́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be transformed, to look different</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преобразование.html>преобразова́ние</a> (7823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразовать.html>преобразова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preobrazovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразование.html>преобразова́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preobrazovánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразование.html>преобразова́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразование.html>преобразова́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразование.html>преобразова́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reform</li>
<li>reformation</li>
<li>transition</li>
<li>transformation, conversion</li>
<li>conversion, translation</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***преобразовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преобразовать.html>преобразова́ть</a> (18893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:образовать.html>образова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obrazovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразовать.html>преобразова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preobrazovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразовать.html>преобразова́ть</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">преобразо́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to transform <i>(into)</i>, to turn <i>(into)</i>, to reform <i>(into)</i>, to reorganize <i>(into, as)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразовать.html>преобразова́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дипломатический.html>дипломати́ческую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:миссия.html>ми́ссию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посольство.html>посо́льство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>preobrazovátʹ</b> diplomatíčeskuju míssiju v posólʹstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to raise/elevate a diplomatic mission to embassy rank</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to transform <i>(into)</i>, to convert <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informatics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to convert <i>(to)</i>, to translate <i>(into)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This verb can be used in the present/future tense as either imperfective or perfective, but in the past and imperative only as perfective.
</p>

***преобразоваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преобразоваться.html>преобразова́ться</a> (29510)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразовать.html>преобразова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preobrazovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразоваться.html>преобразова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preobrazovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразоваться.html>преобразова́ться</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">преобразо́вываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to transform</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reform, to undergo radical change</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be transfigured, to change shape or appearance</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преобразовать.html>преобразова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">preobrazovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This verb can be used in the present/future tense as either imperfective or perfective, but in the past and imperative only as perfective.
</p>

***преодолеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преодолеть.html>преодоле́ть</a> (4265)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолеть.html>одоле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odolétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преодолеть.html>преодоле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preodolétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преодолевать.html>преодолева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get over, to overcome</li>
<li>to traverse</li>
<li>to negotiate</li></ol>
